                     <div data-reactid="805">
                      <div data-reactid="806">
                       Private 400 sqft studio with kitchen,bathroom and separate entrance in beautiful house in a quiet residential neighborhood.Near the beach, Culver City, Playa Vista, Marina Del Rey, Venice Beach, Abbot Kinney.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="807">
                       Private 400 sq ft studio apartment with kitchen, bathroom and separate entrance in beautiful new construction house in quiet residential neighborhood. Near the beach, Culver City, Playa Vista, Mar Vista, Marina Del Rey, Venice beach, the Canals, Abbot Kinney, shopping, art galleries, bike and running path, great restaurants, movie theaters, grocery stores and drug store within a five minute walking distance. Marina Del Rey hospital is 3 minutes away. The airport is 15 minutes away door to door (approximately a $20 cab ride or $12 Uber). Sunny with a nice ocean breeze. Quiet neighborhood. High speed Wi-Fi internet. Hardwood floors, closet and drawers for storage. Full size refrigerator,stove top, microwave, coffee maker, fully equipped kitchen with pots and pans, cutlery, plates, glasses, etc. Full bed with bed linens provided. (Extra guest $30, max 2 guests total.) Full bathroom with “hotel like” amenities and towels. Shared laundry room access with iron and ironing board available to use.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="808">
                       The Del Rey neighborhood is perfectly centrally located on the west side. It is next to Abbot Kinney, Venice Beach and Main Street Santa Monica which are the cool places to be with coffee shops, trendy stores, art galleries, restaurants and bars. The Marina Marketplace is walking distance with two movie theaters, great shops, eateries, super market and 24h pharmacy. Located next to the bike path going straight to the beach. You can keep riding all the way to Santa Monica on the beautiful beach bike path and enjoy the iconic Venice Boardwalk, Santa Monica Pier and Third Street Promenade.
                      </div>

                      <div data-reactid="1770">
                       This is a cozy 1950's built, 2 bedroom 1 bathroom house, with a pleasant, peaceful and private outdoor patio space in the front, and a deck in the back. This home has been renovated with vaulted ceilings, hardwood floors, and french doors.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="1771">
                       Walk through the tall redwood gates of this home and follow the tile path to the front door. To the left before entering the home you see a half circle shaped deck protruding out from the house, and on it a picnic table for meal gatherings in the outdoor. When entering the home you will find yourself in a large open room, much in the style of a studio, where the kitchen, dining room, and living room all share the same space, creating a spacious flow of light, air, and energy. To the left of the entry door, on the same wall you'll find french doors that open out to the front deck, allowing for greater light and air circulation. Down the only hallway to the right is the bathroom, where one can enjoy a relaxing epson salt bath after a long day. On the other side of the hallway you will find the laundry room, which then leads into the master bedroom. Both bedrooms have french doors that open to the back deck. The back deck doesn't feel as private as the front deck, since it boarders my neighbors but is still optimal for lounging. *Bookings run on a first come first serve basis, and no holds are placed until a reservation is paid for.
                      </div>
